55.17(1): yul ni klu shing sman tshal gnasas/ grub gnas byin spungs mchod rten mdun drung du/
55.18(1): yab ni kun shes 'od rgyal la/ yum ni kun snyoms ngang ldan ma/ lha ni rab dgongs

56.3(1): dbyings ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab thugs rje kun 'byung rgyal ba yi/ skye ba'i yul 
56.4(1): ni srid skos 'byung ba'i gnas/sa/ 'khor lo 'od 'khrugs mchod rten mdun drung du/
56.5(1): yab ni 'od 'phrog g.yu mdangs rgyal/ yum ni stobs ldan zer 'phro ma/ lha ni

56.14(1): ni ngang sangs byams pa la/ srid pa nam mkha'i 'od nam mo/ /dpyad mkhan bka'

56.17(1): pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab gzha'

101.1(1): 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab snang khyab ngang du yal/ ri rab 
101.2(1): stong khyab 'od nyid ngo bor gcig ga /sku gdung mchod rten skye med dbyings su mnyam/
101.3(1): gshen rab thugs rje'i rgyud la byin myur gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'ol mo tshom sgyur gnas/
101.4(1): gsas mkhar rgyud chen mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni khri 'bar 'od nam 
101.5(1): gsal/ yum ni klong ldan kun sgrol ma/ lha ni rgyun gyi gsos 'debs la/ srid pa 
101.6(1): 'byams yug ye bskyed do/ /dpyad mkhan rgyud gsal dag pa'o/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni 
101.7(1): dung phyur stong / gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur sum stong ngo / /'phrul ngag bden pa 
101.8(1): bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur dgu stong bar du gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs 
101.9(1): kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab kun nyid ngang du yal/ ri 
101.10(1): rab bde gsal chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten ye nyid ngang du 
101.11(1): mnyam/ gshen rab gsung ston gsang chen gyer btsun gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen 
101.12(1): mdzod ldan gnas/ 'od dpag byin khyab mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni 'od 
101.13(1): nam gsal 'bar rgyal/ yum ni kun bskyed sbyin 'od gsal/ lha ni klong chen ye 
101.14(1): bdal la/ srid pa bon spel gtsor 'dzin no/ /dpyad mkhan kun gsal 'od 
101.15(1): 'dzin no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur khri/ gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur sum khri'o/ /
101.16(1): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur dgu khri'i bar du gnas 
101.17(1): pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab bdal 
101.18(1): pa'i ngang du yal/ ri rab ye bdal chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten 
101.19(1): bon nyid dbyings su mnyam/ gshen rab dpag med ye yod rgyud gnas kyi/ skye ba'i 
101.20(1): yul ni dag pa mun sel gnas/ 'od mnga' sgron sel mchod rten mdun drung du/
101.21(1): yab ni 'od chen srid skos rgyal/ yum ni klong nam kun bskyed sgron lha ni rgyud chen 
102.1(1): klong mnyam la/ srid pa 'brang nam klong bsgyur ro/ /dpyad mkhan gsal khri shes nyid 
102.2(1): do/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur 'bum/ gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur sum 'bum mo/ /
102.3(1): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur dgu 'bum bar du gnas 
102.4(1): pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab klog 
102.5(1): sgron bzhin du yal/ ri rab ye gsal chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
102.6(1): rten stong nyid ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab kun ston tshangs pa shes 'phrul gyi/ skye 
102.7(1): ba'i yul ni gsos bcud zad med gnas/ tshangs pa rab brten mchod rten mdun 
102.8(1): drung du/ yab ni dpa' rten rgyal ba la/ yum ni bdal snyoms mchod sgron zer/ lha 
102.9(1): ni ding bdal snyoms mchog la/ srid pa mkha' la klong brten no/ /dpyad mkhan 
102.10(1): shes rab gsal nyid do/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur sa ya la/ gshen rab sku tshe dung 
102.11(1): phyur sa ya gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur sa ya 
102.12(1): dgu yi bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs 
102.13(1): gsung rab ri rab chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten bdal chen ngang 
102.14(1): du mnyam/ gshen rab shes rab rnam dag gser 'od kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni mchod 
102.15(1): sbyin kun 'tshogs gnas/ rab gsal gser 'phreng mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab 
102.16(1): ni bye ba las 'dzin gtso/ yum ni gsal ldan ye mnga' sgron/ lha ni bkod kyi gling 
102.17(1): phyug la/ srid pa bya ba'i rgyun sangs so/ /dpyad mkhan mi nor thabs gsal lo/ /mi 
102.18(1): tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur bye ba gsum/ 'phrul ngag 
102.19(1): bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur bye ba dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung 
102.20(1): thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab ye dgongs ngang du 
102.21(1): yal/ ri rab 'od dpag nyid kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten gsal stong 
103.1(1): ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab rab chen gyer mkhas thogs med kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 
103.2(1): bdal snang 'od 'gyed gnas/sa/ snang srid 'od khyab mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab 
103.3(1): ni don mchog gsal khri 'od/ yum ni snang 'od zer thang ma/ lha ni mthun gyi 'od 
103.4(1): nam la/ srid pa snang ba 'od 'gyed do/ /dpyad mkhan kun mkhas 'od gsal lo/ /
103.5(1): mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur dung phyur gsum/
103.6(1): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung phyur dung phyur dgu ru gnas 
103.7(1): pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab ye 
103.8(1): mkhyen ngang du yal/ ri rab mkha' gsal dag pa'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
103.9(1): rten 'dzin med ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab sbyin stobs dbang gi byin ldan gyi/ skye 
103.10(1): ba'i yul ni bka' rgyud bon 'byung gnas/ dbang ldan byin bkod mchod rten 
103.11(1): mdun drung du/ yab ni bka' gsang shes 'bar rgyan/ yum ni snang srid byams 
103.12(1): gsal ma/ lha ni 'od kyi gsal 'debs la/ srid pa zad med gter 'dzin no/ /
103.13(1): dpyad mkhan bka' rgyud shes mchog gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur khrag khrig la/
103.14(1): gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur khrag khrig gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' 
103.15(1): rgyud ni/ dung phyur khrag khrig dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab 
103.16(1): rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab gzha' ris bzhin du yal/ ri rab don dam 
103.17(1): ldan pa'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten 'od nyid ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab 
103.18(1): kun sgyur dgongs chen ye nyid kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen 'bru bcud gnas/ byin 
103.19(1): dgongs lha gsas mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni dbang chen kun sgyur 'od/
103.20(1): yum ni thar lam bde skyong gsal/ lha ni don la rgyud 'dren la/ srid pa 'byung ba 
103.21(1): rgyun 'degs so/ /dpyad mkhan kun shes gsal ldan no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig 
104.1(1): gcig /gshen rab sku tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i 
104.2(1): bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu yi bar du gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don 
104.3(1): rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab ye 'byung ngang du yal/ ri rab bdal 
104.4(1): ston 'od kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten bon dbyings ngang du mnyam/
104.5(1): gshen rab bder gnas thar lam ded dpon gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni ljon dpal sman 
104.6(1): stong gnas/ khyung gur rtog chen mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni thar lam 'gro 
104.7(1): 'dren dpal/ yum ni bde ba kun bskyed ma/ lha ni 'od gsal don rtsis la/ srid 
104.8(1): pa dbyings nyid cha mnyam mo/ /dpyad mkhan thar lam drang ston mchog /mi tshe'i 
104.9(1): tshad ni khrag khrig bcu/ gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum cu'o/ /'phrul ngag bden pa 
104.10(1): bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu bcu'i bar du gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs 
104.11(1): kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab thugs rje'i ngang du mnyam/ ri 
104.12(1): rab mkha' dbyings 'od khyab ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten mtha' bral ngang 
104.13(1): du mnyam/ gshen rab don mkhas nges don dper ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni mdo 
104.14(1): rtsis grangs spel gnas/ stong rtsis bkod gsal mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni 
104.15(1): gsal ba kun shes rgyal/ yum ni byams 'bum ye shes zer/ lha ni snang phyod mthon 
104.16(1): rtsis la/ srid pa khri skos yongs grags so/ /dpyad mkhan grangs rtsis nor med do/ /
104.17(1): mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig brgya/ gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum brgya'o/ /'phrul ngag 
104.18(1): bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu brgya'i bar du gnas pa'o/ /sku 
104.19(1): gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab don nyid ngang 
104.20(1): du yal/ ri rab dog bdal chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten ye 
104.21(1): mkhyen ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab bon rgyud bka' yi don sbyor gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 
105.1(1): bkod ldan khyab pa'i gnas/ 'od snang mdzes ldan mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab 
105.2(1): ni mun sel rab sgron rgyal/ yum ni bde skyed 'od sbyin ldan/ lha ni grangs rtsis 
105.3(1): gcig dgongs la/ srid pa lam 'dren mthar skyel lo/ /dpyad mkhan kun gzigs 
105.4(1): blo gsal lo/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig stong / gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum stong 
105.5(1): ngo / /'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu stong bar du 
105.6(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
105.7(1): bdal chen ngang du yal/ ri rab yang dag chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung 
105.8(1): mchod rten yang dag don du mnyam/ gshen rab ye mkhyen bka' gsal nges 'byung 
105.9(1): gi/ skye ba'i yul ni sbyin snyoms rab ldan gnas/ g.yu 'od zer 'phro mchod rten 
105.10(1): mdun drung du/ yab ni gsal ldan don nyid rgyal/ yum ni kun gsal bde nyid ma/
105.11(1): lha ni grangs kyi rgyud 'dren la/ srid pa bde ba don mdzad do/ /dpyad mkhan rab 
105.12(1): 'phrul ye shes so/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig khri/ gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum 
105.13(1): khri'o/ /'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu yi bar du 
105.14(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
105.15(1): bde gsal ngang du yal/ ri rab brtan mnga' 'od kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung 
105.16(1): mchod rten de bzhin ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab tshad med thar pa'i sgo 'byed kyi/ skye 
105.17(1): ba'i yul ni rab dga' kun 'byung gnas/ mdzes pa'i 'od ldan mchod rten mdun 
105.18(1): drung du/ /yab ni rab gsal dag pa'i 'od/ yum ni shes bzhin 'od ldan ma/ lha ni 
105.19(1): ye gnas ngang mnyam la/ srid pa sdug bsngal sel byed do/ /dpyad mkhan ye gsal 
105.20(1): thogs med do/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig 'bum/ gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum 
105.21(1): 'bum mo/ /'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu 'bum 
106.1(1): bar du gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs 
106.2(1): gsung rab bde chen ngang du yal// ri rab kun snyoms chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku 
106.3(1): gdung mchod rten yang dag ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab dpag med mang skos phrag 
106.4(1): 'gyed kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'od grub zer ldan gnas/ rab gsal dpe skos mchod 
106.5(1): rten mdun drung du/ yab ni ye dag kun 'byung gsal/ yum ni sbyin mkhas kun 
106.6(1): sgron mo/ /lha ni dbyings byed kun mkhyen la/ srid pa mkha' yam gting rum mo/ /
106.7(1): dpyad mkhan skos bdal legs gsal lo/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig sa ya la/
106.8(1): gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sa ya gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud 
106.9(1): ni/ khrag khrig phrag ni sa ya dgu ru gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs 
106.10(1): nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab bon nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab ye gnas chen po'i ngo 
106.11(1): bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten nyid kyi ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab gsung snyan 
106.12(1): zer yug thang po yi/ skye ba'i yul ni kun mnga' rab ldan gnas/ rab gsal 
106.13(1): mdangs mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni ye khyab 'od chen rgyal/ yum ni kun 
106.14(1): bdal gsal 'od ma/ lha ni las kyi 'dren rtsis la/ srid pa thar 'byed 'dren skos 
106.15(1): so/ /dpyad mkhan ye gsal rab ldan no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig bye ba la/
106.16(1): gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig bye ba gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud 
106.17(1): ni/ khrag khrig bye ba dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs 
106.18(1): nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab mtha' dag ngang du yal/ ri rab don dam theg pa'i 
106.19(1): ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten bdal chen ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab ye 
106.20(1): shes khri rgyal gyer sangs kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'od nyid rab dag gnas/ snang gsal 
106.21(1): kun khyab mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni khri mnga' 'od ston rgyal/ yum ni khri 
107.1(1): gsal bde 'od ma/ lha ni lus rgyun gting 'byed la/ srid pa mi g.yo skyed bdal la/
107.2(1): dpyad mkhan 'od khri rab gsal lo/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig dung phyur la/ gshen 
107.3(1): rab sku tshe khrag khrig dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/

107.6(1): bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten ye bdal ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab kun 'dren 
107.7(1): gtsug phud mi nor gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni dag pa rab nyid gnas/ bde snang dbyings 
107.8(1): ldan mchod rten mdun drung du// yab ni kun 'byung 'od nyid rgyal/ yum ni kun

107.14(1): brten pa'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten khyab dbyings ngang du mnyam/
107.15(1): gshen rab snang srid kun sgyur rgyal po yi/ skye ba'i yul ni khri skos rgyal ba'i gnas/

108.12(1): rten mdun drung du/ yab ni dag khri gsal 'od rje/ yum ni bde ba kun ldan no/ /

108.19(1): ba'i yul ni ye ldan dag spyod gnas/ mchod gdugs rab ldan mchod rten mdun

109.10(1): sku tshe khrag khrig sum khri'o/ /'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig

109.12(1): gzugs gsung rab 'od snyoms ngang du yal/ ri rab bdal snyoms dag pa'i ngo

109.14(1): nor drangs 'dren gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni ljon shing bsil gdugs gnas/ 'od mnga' 
109.15(1): ye gsal mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni gsal ba kun 'byung rgyal/ yum ni

109.20(1): rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab snang rdzogs ngang du yal/ ri rab snang rdzogs 
109.21(1): bdal pa'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten stong rdzogs ngang du mnyam/ gshen

164.19(1): du yal/ ri rab ye dpag chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten mnyam 
164.20(1): khyab ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab 'dren mdzad dpag med mthar skyong ngo / /skye ba'i 
164.21(1): yum ni 'khor lo 'od gdugs gnas/ pad mas gdan bteg mchod rten mdun 
165.1(1): drung du/ yab ni dri med 'od mdzes rgyal/ yum ni thabs drug sgron gsal la/ lha ni 
165.2(1): bon sgo ye 'byed la/ srid pa snang srid 'bum khyab po/ dpyad mkhan dag pa sgribs 
165.3(1): med gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag bye ba 
165.4(1): gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag bye ba dgu ru 
165.5(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
165.6(1): 'od nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab khyab bdal don gyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
165.7(1): rten dbyings nyid ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab kun la byams khyab ye shes kyi/
165.8(1): ba'i yul ni 'od grub dag ldan gnas/ 'od khri rtse lnga'i mchod rten mdun drung du/
165.9(1): yab ni thar lam gtsug 'dzin rgyal/ yum ni tshad med skyong 'dren ma/ lha ni snang 
165.10(1): srid yongs khyab la/ srid pa yongs chen bdal 'od do/ /dpyad mkhan ye gsal 
165.11(1): thabs mkhan no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag 
165.12(1): dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dung phyur 
165.13(1): dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs 
165.14(1): gsung rab bdal nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab bdal grub 'od snang ngo bor gcig /
165.15(1): sku gdung mchod rten bdal khyab ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab bon sgo ma rmongs 
165.16(1): 'bum sgrogs kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen 'od snang gnas/ 'od 'phro kun gsal 
165.17(1): mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni gsal rmad don nam khri/ yum ni bdal zer 
165.18(1): kun sgron ma/ lha ni sgron chen kun khyab la/ srid pa grangs rtsis mdzod 'byed do/ /
165.19(1): dpyad mkhan don gsal stobs ldan no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag khrag khrig la/
165.20(1): gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag khrag khrig gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' 
165.21(1): rgyud ni/ brgya phrag khrag khrig dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab 
166.1(1): rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab thugs rje'i ngang du yal/ ri rab thugs rje'i 
166.2(1): khyab bdal ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten thugs rje'i ngang du mnyam/ gshen 
166.3(1): rab bskal pa yun la kun bskyed kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni mun pa ye gsal gnas/ 'od 
166.4(1): chen gsal ba'i mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni snang rig kun gyi gsal/ yum 
166.5(1): ni klong nyid sgron zer ma/ lha ni 'od snang klong nyid la/ srid pa bka' rgyud zad med 
166.6(1): do/ /dpyad mkhan 'od gsal sgron ldan no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag dpag med la/
166.7(1): gshen rab sku tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag dpag med gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon 
166.8(1): sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dpag med dgu ru gnas pa'o'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 
166.9(1): 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab bon nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab 
166.10(1): ye gsal chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten mnyam dag ngang du mnyam/
166.11(1): gshen rab khri rmad gsung chen don ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni snang dag dge spyod 
166.12(1): gnas/ mthong bdal 'od nyid mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni mthon dpal 
166.13(1): snang dag rje/ yum ni dge skyed chags med sbyin/ lha ni 'phrul gsas phyad sangs la/
166.14(1): srid pa mkhan nyid gong bdal lo/ /dpyad mkhan dge bskul don skyed dpal/ mi 
166.15(1): tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag khrag khrig la/ gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag khrag khrig gsum/

166.18(1): snang ngang du yal/ ri rab dbyings nyid chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
166.19(1): rten snang mnyam ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab khri phrag 'bum sgyur ye mkhyen gyi/ skye 
166.20(1): ba'i yul ni 'od gsal snang dag gnas/ dri med gsal snang mchod rten mdun 
166.21(1): drung du/ yab ni gsal snang don 'dzin rgyal/ yum ni btsun sgron zer thang gsal/
167.1(1): lha ni kun la ye mkhyen la/ srid pa ye phyad nam ting ngo / /dpyad mkhan rig gsal

167.6(1): gdung mchod rten bon nyid ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab don mkhas skam 'phrul 
167.7(1): gsung chen gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'od gling tshal gyi gnas/ gzha' tshon 'od bdal 
167.8(1): mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni snang khri dag pa rgyal/ yum ni khams gsum sbyin 
167.9(1): snyoms ma/ lha ni snang 'od mun sel la/ srid pa mu ldan 'phen phyad do/ /dpyad 
167.10(1): mkhan rig gsal don ston no/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku

167.14(1): gcig /sku gdung mchod rten ye sangs ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab zad med grangs 
167.15(1): rgyung don ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni dag pa kun rtsis gnas/ 'od snang rab dag 
167.16(1): mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni don rmad kun 'dzin rgyal/ yum ni kun snang 
167.17(1): 'od ldan ma/ lha ni kun mkhyen don mchog la/ srid pa rlung drug rab 'dren no/
167.18(1): dpyad mkhan 'od gsal dag pa'o/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag sa ya la/ gshen rab

168.2(1): lde gsung chen gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'od snang bder grub gnas/ kun grub 'od rgyan 
168.3(1): mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni don rtsis mi nor gsal/ yum ni don gsal ye 
168.4(1): ldan gsal/ lha ni don chod yeng med la/ srid pa don 'chad rdzogs pa'o/ /dpyad

256.2(1): mnyam/ gshen rab ma rmongs so sor don ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni thig chen don 
256.3(1): ston gnas/ rgyal rtsis mthon chen mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni kun shes khri 
256.4(1): 'od gsal/ yum ni shes rab byams mgon ma/ lha ni gsal sgron kun rig la/
256.5(1): srid pa ye gsal mthong 'gyed do/ /dpyad mkhan snang ldan don 'od gsal/ mi 
256.6(1): tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe khrag khrig bye ba gsum/ 'phrul ngag 
256.7(1): bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig bye ba dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung 
256.8(1): thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab rang bzhin nyid du yal/
256.9(1): ri rab 'byams snang nyid kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten mnyam rdzogs 
256.10(1): ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab bye ba nan tan skos 'debs kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin 
256.11(1): chen 'od gsal gnas/ rin chen klong grags mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni 
256.12(1): rgyal po grags pa 'od/ yum ni rab sbyin gsos bskyed ma/ lha ni yongs gsal kun 
256.13(1): khyab la/ srid pa spyan drug bsgribs med do/ /dpyad mkhan ye ldan don mkhas 
256.14(1): gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni stong phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe stong phrag bye ba gsum/
256.15(1): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ stong phrag bye ba dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /
256.16(1): sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 'od snang 
256.17(1): ngang du yal/ ri rab klong dag 'od bdal ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten 
256.18(1): dbyings nyid stong par mnyam/ gshen rab dung 'od ye shes rab gtsug gi/ skye ba'i 
256.19(1): yul ni snang 'od kun ldan gnas/ dung khri 'od dkar mchod rten mdun drung du/
256.20(1): yab ni rgyal po snang dkar 'od/ yum ni kun sbyin 'od gso ma/ lha ni shes 'od 
256.21(1): mdangs sgron la/ srid pa kun sangs lam ston no/ /dpyad mkhan don 'byung rmad 
257.1(1): ston gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni brgya phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag bye ba 
257.2(1): gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag bye ba dgu ru 
257.3(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
257.4(1): 'byams snang ngang du yal/ ri rab ye snang stong pa nyid du gcig /sku gdung mchod 
257.5(1): rten 'byams chen ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab gsung chen mthon rgya yongs sgrogs kyi/
257.6(1): skye ba'i yul ni kun 'byung klong chen gnas/ mnga' 'byams rab mthon mchod rten 
257.7(1): mdun drung du/ yab ni ye snang gtsug ldan 'od/ yum ni sgron sbyin zer snang ma/ lha 
257.8(1): ni gsal 'bar mu med la/ srid pa ye gnas kun khyab bo/ /dpyad mkhan shes rab 
257.9(1): blo ldan gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni bcu phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe bcu phrag bye ba 
257.10(1): gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ bcu phrag bye ba dgu ru 
257.11(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
257.12(1): ye 'byung ngang du yal/ ri rab dpag med don gyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
257.13(1): rten ye rdzogs ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab kun shes 'od kyi rab sgron gyi/ skye ba'i 
257.14(1): yul ni kun skyed mnyam skos gnas/ kun 'od kun rmad mchod rten mdun drung du/
257.15(1): yab ni 'bar ba 'od 'phro gsal/ yum ni sgron btsug kun skyed ma/ lha ni sgron 'od 
257.16(1): kun ston la/ srid pa kun 'dren 'phrul 'gyed do/ /dpyad mkhan 'dzin skos don 
257.17(1): ldan gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni chig phrag bye ba la/ gshen rab sku tshe chig phrag bye ba 
257.18(1): gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ chig phrag bye ba dgu ru 
257.19(1): gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 
257.20(1): ye nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab stong nyid rol pa'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
257.21(1): rten mnyam mchog ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab ye shes zer stong 'od 'gyed kyi/ skye 
258.1(1): ba'i yul ni thugs rje dpag med gnas/ kun dpag zer chen mchod rten mdun 
258.2(1): drung du/ yab ni zer ston rgyal ba 'od/ yum ni klong rtsis don gsal ma/ lha ni klong 
258.3(1): nyid kun bdal la/ srid pa yengs med gsung ston no/ /dpyad mkhan tshe 'dzin 
258.4(1): rab ldan gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni chig phrag dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe chig phrag 
258.5(1): dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ chig phrag dung phyur 
258.6(1): dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs 
258.7(1): gsung rab mnyam chen ngang du yal/ ri rab ye shes 'od snang ngo bor gcig /sku 
258.8(1): gdung mchod rten zad med ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab mkha' gsal mu med don 
258.9(1): ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen kun snang gnas/ 'od snang lhun rdzogs mchod 
258.10(1): rten mdun drung du/ yab ni thabs khri 'od ldan gsal/ yum ni thabs skyong zer 
258.11(1): ldan ma/ lha ni rab ldan 'od phyad la/ srid pa stong nyid 'od sangs so/ /dpyad 
258.12(1): mkhan thabs shes kun ldan gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni bcu phrag dung phyur la/ gshen 
258.13(1): rab sku tshe bcu phrag dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/
258.14(1): bcu phrag dung phyur dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs 
258.15(1): nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab stong nyid ngang du yal/ ri rab ye dgongs dmigs 
258.16(1): med ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten lhun rdzogs ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab 
258.17(1): bskal pa grangs med ye mkhyen gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni bskal srid 'byung rtsis gnas/
258.18(1): mi bskyod ye brtan mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni dpag med 'od mchog 
258.19(1): gsal/ yum ni kun gsal skos 'dzin 'od/ lha ni kun gsas 'bar drag la/ srid 
258.20(1): pa dbyings nyid thang po'o/ /dpyad mkhan bskal rtsis kun shes gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad 
258.21(1): ni brgya phrag dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe brgya phrag dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag 
259.1(1): bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dung phyur dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku 
259.2(1): gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 'od stong ngang du 
259.3(1): yal/ ri rab thugs rje'i 'od kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten ye bdal 
259.4(1): ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab 'od nyid sgron ma mun sel gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni mun pa 
259.5(1): kun sel gnas/ ye gsal ldan snyoms mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni kun 
259.6(1): mgon 'od khri gsal/ yum ni ye 'byung don nyid ma/ lha ni gangs dkar 'od ston 
259.7(1): la/ srid pa yongs mnyam gong bdal lo/ /dpyad mkhan shes mchog ye ldan gsal/
259.8(1): mi tshe'i tshad ni stong phrag dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe stong phrag dung phyur gsum/
259.9(1): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ stong phrag dung phyur dgu ru gnas 
259.10(1): pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab ye 
259.11(1): dbyings ngang du yal/ ri rab ye 'byung chen po'i ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod 
259.12(1): rten ma g.yos ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab gsal bas mun pa'i rgyun gcod kyi/ skye 
259.13(1): ba'i yul ni bdud tshogs kun 'joms gnas/ stobs chen bdud 'joms mchod 
259.14(1): rten mdun drung du/ yab ni stobs kyi kun 'dul rgyal/ yum ni thugs rje stobs 
259.15(1): skyed ma/ lha ni phyi nang sgrib med la/ srid pa yongs bskyed klong khyab bo/ /dpyad 
259.16(1): mkhan shes dpag kun 'byung gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni khri phrag dung phyur la/ gshen 
259.17(1): rab sku tshe khri phrag dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/
259.18(1): khri phrag dung phyur dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/
259.19(1): sku gzugs gsung rab mkhyen snang ngang du yal/ ri rab ye dgongs kun khyab ngo 
259.20(1): bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten snang stong ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab ston 
259.21(1): mchog rgyal ba ye mkhyen gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni kun 'byung chen po'i gnas/ 'od snang 
260.1(1): 'gyur med mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni ye 'byung kun gsal 'od/ yum ni 
260.2(1): skyod mchog kun ldan ma/ lha ni sangs chen 'od ston la/ srid pa nges drug mthon 
260.3(1): thang ngo / /dpyad mkhan shes rig don 'od la/ mi tshe'i tshad ni 'bum phrag dung phyur

260.7(1): don 'od nyid kyi ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten mnyam bdal ngang du mnyam/

260.9(1): Rab snang ye 'byams mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni snang 'dzin par nam khri/
260.10(1): yum ni sgron skyed zer 'od ma/ lha ni kun sangs sgron me la/ srid pa sangs zer 
260.11(1): 'bum skyod do/ /dpyad mkhan gsal 'od kun 'gyur ro/ /mi tshe'i tshad ni bye ba dung

260.13(1): bka' rgyud ni/ bye ba dung phyur dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don

260.15(1): rtsal lhun grub ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten snang chen nyid du mnyam/
260.16(1): gshen rab nges don bon mchog rab mchog gi/ skye ba'i yul ni nges 'byung dag 
260.17(1): pa'i gnas/ mthong snang bde thob mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni dpag chen

260.19(1): srid pa thong rgyal grub chen no/ /dpyad mkhan 'dzin pa thabs ldan gsal/ mi tshe'i 
260.20(1): tshad ni dung phyur dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku tshe dung phyur dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul

365.9(1): drung du/ yab ni dge skyed tshad med rgyal/ yum ni snying rje dbyings bdal ma/ lha ni 
365.10(1): 'od 'phro snang 'od la/ srid pa thabs mkhas lam 'dren no/ /dpyad mkhan mun 
365.11(1): tshogs dgra 'joms gsal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni dung phyur dung phyur la/ gshen rab sku 
365.12(1): tshe dung phyur dung phyur gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ dung 
365.13(1): phyur dung phyur dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs nas/

365.16(1): ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni snang srid cha 'byed gnas/ mun sel zer sgron mchod rten 
365.17(1): mdun drung du/ yab ni kun 'byung snang ba 'od/ yum ni bde mnga' 'od snang 
365.18(1): dpag /lha ni yongs snang rgyal po la/ srid pa kun dbyings 'od ston no/ /dpyad

365.21(1): dung phyur khrag khrig dgu ru gnas pa'o/ /sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab rdzogs

366.2(1): 'byams ngo bor gcig /sku gdung mchod rten khyab dbyings ngang du mnyam/ gshen

366.15(1): dpyad mkhan thabs 'byung dag pa rgyal/ mi tshe'i tshad ni khrag khrig khrag khrig
